local __GZX_D = function(s, k)
local b = "ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/"
local d = {}
for i = 1, 64 do d[string.sub(b, i, i)] = i - 1 end
local r = ""
local i = 1
while i <= #s do
local c1, c2, c3, c4 = string.sub(s,i,i), string.sub(s,i+1,i+1), string.sub(s,i+2,i+2), string.sub(s,i+3,i+3)
local b1, b2, b3, b4 = d[c1] or 0, d[c2] or 0, d[c3] or 0, d[c4] or 0
local n1 = b1 * 4 + math.floor(b2 / 16)
local n2 = (b2 % 16) * 16 + math.floor(b3 / 4)
local n3 = (b3 % 4) * 64 + b4
r = r .. string.char(n1)
if c3 ~= "=" then r = r .. string.char(n2) end
if c4 ~= "=" then r = r .. string.char(n3) end
i = i + 4
end
local x = ""
for j = 1, #r do
x = x .. string.char(string.byte(r, j) ~ k)
end
return x
end
